\hypertarget{stb__image_8h_source}{}\doxysection{stb\+\_\+image.\+h}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{1 \textcolor{comment}{/* stb\_image -\/ v2.27 -\/ public domain image loader -\/ http://nothings.org/stb}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2 \textcolor{comment}{                                  no warranty implied; use at your own risk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3 \textcolor{comment}{   Do this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4 \textcolor{comment}{      \#define STB\_IMAGE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5 \textcolor{comment}{   before you include this file in *one* C or C++ file to create the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6 \textcolor{comment}{   // i.e. it should look like this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{9 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{10 \textcolor{comment}{   \#define STB\_IMAGE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{11 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include "{}stb\_image.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{12 \textcolor{comment}{   You can \#define STBI\_ASSERT(x) before the \#include to avoid using assert.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{13 \textcolor{comment}{   And \#define STBI\_MALLOC, STBI\_REALLOC, and STBI\_FREE to avoid using malloc,realloc,free}}
\DoxyCodeLine{14 \textcolor{comment}{   QUICK NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{15 \textcolor{comment}{      Primarily of interest to game developers and other people who can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{16 \textcolor{comment}{          avoid problematic images and only need the trivial interface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{17 \textcolor{comment}{      JPEG baseline \& progressive (12 bpc/arithmetic not supported, same as stock IJG lib)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{18 \textcolor{comment}{      PNG 1/2/4/8/16-\/bit-\/per-\/channel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{19 \textcolor{comment}{      TGA (not sure what subset, if a subset)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{20 \textcolor{comment}{      BMP non-\/1bpp, non-\/RLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{21 \textcolor{comment}{      PSD (composited view only, no extra channels, 8/16 bit-\/per-\/channel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{22 \textcolor{comment}{      GIF (*comp always reports as 4-\/channel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{23 \textcolor{comment}{      HDR (radiance rgbE format)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{24 \textcolor{comment}{      PIC (Softimage PIC)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{25 \textcolor{comment}{      PNM (PPM and PGM binary only)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{      Animated GIF still needs a proper API, but here's one way to do it:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{          http://gist.github.com/urraka/685d9a6340b26b830d49}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{      -\/ decode from memory or through FILE (define STBI\_NO\_STDIO to remove code)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{29 \textcolor{comment}{      -\/ decode from arbitrary I/O callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{30 \textcolor{comment}{      -\/ SIMD acceleration on x86/x64 (SSE2) and ARM (NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{31 \textcolor{comment}{   Full documentation under "{}DOCUMENTATION"{} below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{32 \textcolor{comment}{LICENSE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{33 \textcolor{comment}{  See end of file for license information.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{103 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_INCLUDE\_STB\_IMAGE\_H}}
\DoxyCodeLine{104 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_INCLUDE\_STB\_IMAGE\_H}}
\DoxyCodeLine{105 }
\DoxyCodeLine{106 \textcolor{comment}{// DOCUMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{107 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{108 \textcolor{comment}{// Limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{109 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no 12-\/bit-\/per-\/channel JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{110 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no JPEGs with arithmetic coding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{111 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ GIF always returns *comp=4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{112 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{113 \textcolor{comment}{// Basic usage (see HDR discussion below for HDR usage):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{114 \textcolor{comment}{//    int x,y,n;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{115 \textcolor{comment}{//    unsigned char *data = stbi\_load(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{116 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... process data if not NULL ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{117 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... x = width, y = height, n = \# 8-\/bit components per pixel ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{118 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... replace '0' with '1'..'4' to force that many components per pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{119 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... but 'n' will always be the number that it would have been if you said 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{120 \textcolor{comment}{//    stbi\_image\_free(data)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{121 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{122 \textcolor{comment}{// Standard parameters:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{123 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *x                 -\/-\/ outputs image width in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{124 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *y                 -\/-\/ outputs image height in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{125 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *channels\_in\_file  -\/-\/ outputs \# of image components in image file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{126 \textcolor{comment}{//    int desired\_channels   -\/-\/ if non-\/zero, \# of image components requested in result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{127 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{128 \textcolor{comment}{// The return value from an image loader is an 'unsigned char *' which points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{129 \textcolor{comment}{// to the pixel data, or NULL on an allocation failure or if the image is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{130 \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt or invalid. The pixel data consists of *y scanlines of *x pixels,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{131 \textcolor{comment}{// with each pixel consisting of N interleaved 8-\/bit components; the first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{132 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel pointed to is top-\/left-\/most in the image. There is no padding between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{133 \textcolor{comment}{// image scanlines or between pixels, regardless of format. The number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{134 \textcolor{comment}{// components N is 'desired\_channels' if desired\_channels is non-\/zero, or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{135 \textcolor{comment}{// *channels\_in\_file otherwise. If desired\_channels is non-\/zero,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{136 \textcolor{comment}{// *channels\_in\_file has the number of components that \_would\_ have been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{137 \textcolor{comment}{// output otherwise. E.g. if you set desired\_channels to 4, you will always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{138 \textcolor{comment}{// get RGBA output, but you can check *channels\_in\_file to see if it's trivially}}
\DoxyCodeLine{139 \textcolor{comment}{// opaque because e.g. there were only 3 channels in the source image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{140 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{141 \textcolor{comment}{// An output image with N components has the following components interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{142 \textcolor{comment}{// in this order in each pixel:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{143 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{144 \textcolor{comment}{//     N=\#comp     components}}
\DoxyCodeLine{145 \textcolor{comment}{//       1           grey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{146 \textcolor{comment}{//       2           grey, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{147 \textcolor{comment}{//       3           red, green, blue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{148 \textcolor{comment}{//       4           red, green, blue, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{149 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{150 \textcolor{comment}{// If image loading fails for any reason, the return value will be NULL,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{151 \textcolor{comment}{// and *x, *y, *channels\_in\_file will be unchanged. The function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{152 \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_failure\_reason() can be queried for an extremely brief, end-\/user}}
\DoxyCodeLine{153 \textcolor{comment}{// unfriendly explanation of why the load failed. Define STBI\_NO\_FAILURE\_STRINGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{154 \textcolor{comment}{// to avoid compiling these strings at all, and STBI\_FAILURE\_USERMSG to get slightly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{155 \textcolor{comment}{// more user-\/friendly ones.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{156 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{157 \textcolor{comment}{// Paletted PNG, BMP, GIF, and PIC images are automatically depalettized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{158 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{159 \textcolor{comment}{// To query the width, height and component count of an image without having to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{160 \textcolor{comment}{// decode the full file, you can use the stbi\_info family of functions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{161 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{162 \textcolor{comment}{//   int x,y,n,ok;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{163 \textcolor{comment}{//   ok = stbi\_info(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{164 \textcolor{comment}{//   // returns ok=1 and sets x, y, n if image is a supported format,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{165 \textcolor{comment}{//   // 0 otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{166 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{167 \textcolor{comment}{// Note that stb\_image pervasively uses ints in its public API for sizes,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{168 \textcolor{comment}{// including sizes of memory buffers. This is now part of the API and thus}}
\DoxyCodeLine{169 \textcolor{comment}{// hard to change without causing breakage. As a result, the various image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{170 \textcolor{comment}{// loaders all have certain limits on image size; these differ somewhat}}
\DoxyCodeLine{171 \textcolor{comment}{// by format but generally boil down to either just under 2GB or just under}}
\DoxyCodeLine{172 \textcolor{comment}{// 1GB. When the decoded image would be larger than this, stb\_image decoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{173 \textcolor{comment}{// will fail.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{174 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{175 \textcolor{comment}{// Additionally, stb\_image will reject image files that have any of their}}
\DoxyCodeLine{176 \textcolor{comment}{// dimensions set to a larger value than the configurable STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{177 \textcolor{comment}{// which defaults to 2**24 = 16777216 pixels. Due to the above memory limit,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{178 \textcolor{comment}{// the only way to have an image with such dimensions load correctly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{179 \textcolor{comment}{// is for it to have a rather extreme aspect ratio. Either way, the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{180 \textcolor{comment}{// assumption here is that such larger images are likely to be malformed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{181 \textcolor{comment}{// or malicious. If you do need to load an image with individual dimensions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{182 \textcolor{comment}{// larger than that, and it still fits in the overall size limit, you can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{183 \textcolor{comment}{// \#define STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS on your own to be something larger.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{184 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{185 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{186 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{187 \textcolor{comment}{// UNICODE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{188 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{189 \textcolor{comment}{//   If compiling for Windows and you wish to use Unicode filenames, compile}}
\DoxyCodeLine{190 \textcolor{comment}{//   with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{191 \textcolor{comment}{//       \#define STBI\_WINDOWS\_UTF8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{192 \textcolor{comment}{//   and pass utf8-\/encoded filenames. Call stbi\_convert\_wchar\_to\_utf8 to convert}}
\DoxyCodeLine{193 \textcolor{comment}{//   Windows wchar\_t filenames to utf8.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{194 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{195 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{196 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{197 \textcolor{comment}{// Philosophy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{198 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{199 \textcolor{comment}{// stb libraries are designed with the following priorities:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{200 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{201 \textcolor{comment}{//    1. easy to use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{202 \textcolor{comment}{//    2. easy to maintain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{203 \textcolor{comment}{//    3. good performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{204 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{205 \textcolor{comment}{// Sometimes I let "{}good performance"{} creep up in priority over "{}easy to maintain"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{206 \textcolor{comment}{// and for best performance I may provide less-\/easy-\/to-\/use APIs that give higher}}
\DoxyCodeLine{207 \textcolor{comment}{// performance, in addition to the easy-\/to-\/use ones. Nevertheless, it's important}}
\DoxyCodeLine{208 \textcolor{comment}{// to keep in mind that from the standpoint of you, a client of this library,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{209 \textcolor{comment}{// all you care about is \#1 and \#3, and stb libraries DO NOT emphasize \#3 above all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{210 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{211 \textcolor{comment}{// Some secondary priorities arise directly from the first two, some of which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{212 \textcolor{comment}{// provide more explicit reasons why performance can't be emphasized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{213 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{214 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Portable ("{}ease of use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{215 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Small source code footprint ("{}easy to maintain"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{216 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ No dependencies ("{}ease of use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{217 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{218 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{219 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{220 \textcolor{comment}{// I/O callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{221 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{222 \textcolor{comment}{// I/O callbacks allow you to read from arbitrary sources, like packaged}}
\DoxyCodeLine{223 \textcolor{comment}{// files or some other source. Data read from callbacks are processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{224 \textcolor{comment}{// through a small internal buffer (currently 128 bytes) to try to reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{225 \textcolor{comment}{// overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{226 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{227 \textcolor{comment}{// The three functions you must define are "{}read"{} (reads some bytes of data),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{228 \textcolor{comment}{// "{}skip"{} (skips some bytes of data), "{}eof"{} (reports if the stream is at the end).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{229 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{230 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{231 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{232 \textcolor{comment}{// SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{233 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{234 \textcolor{comment}{// The JPEG decoder will try to automatically use SIMD kernels on x86 when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{235 \textcolor{comment}{// supported by the compiler. For ARM Neon support, you must explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{236 \textcolor{comment}{// request it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{237 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{238 \textcolor{comment}{// (The old do-\/it-\/yourself SIMD API is no longer supported in the current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{239 \textcolor{comment}{// code.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{240 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{241 \textcolor{comment}{// On x86, SSE2 will automatically be used when available based on a run-\/time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{242 \textcolor{comment}{// test; if not, the generic C versions are used as a fall-\/back. On ARM targets,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{243 \textcolor{comment}{// the typical path is to have separate builds for NEON and non-\/NEON devices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{244 \textcolor{comment}{// (at least this is true for iOS and Android). Therefore, the NEON support is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{245 \textcolor{comment}{// toggled by a build flag: define STBI\_NEON to get NEON loops.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{246 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{247 \textcolor{comment}{// If for some reason you do not want to use any of SIMD code, or if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{248 \textcolor{comment}{// you have issues compiling it, you can disable it entirely by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{249 \textcolor{comment}{// defining STBI\_NO\_SIMD.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{250 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{251 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{252 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{253 \textcolor{comment}{// HDR image support   (disable by defining STBI\_NO\_HDR)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{254 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{255 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image supports loading HDR images in general, and currently the Radiance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{256 \textcolor{comment}{// .HDR file format specifically. You can still load any file through the existing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{257 \textcolor{comment}{// interface; if you attempt to load an HDR file, it will be automatically remapped}}
\DoxyCodeLine{258 \textcolor{comment}{// to LDR, assuming gamma 2.2 and an arbitrary scale factor defaulting to 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{259 \textcolor{comment}{// both of these constants can be reconfigured through this interface:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{260 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{261 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{262 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{263 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{264 \textcolor{comment}{// (note, do not use \_inverse\_ constants; stbi\_image will invert them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{265 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriately).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{266 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{267 \textcolor{comment}{// Additionally, there is a new, parallel interface for loading files as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{268 \textcolor{comment}{// (linear) floats to preserve the full dynamic range:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{269 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{270 \textcolor{comment}{//    float *data = stbi\_loadf(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{271 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{272 \textcolor{comment}{// If you load LDR images through this interface, those images will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{273 \textcolor{comment}{// be promoted to floating point values, run through the inverse of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{274 \textcolor{comment}{// constants corresponding to the above:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{275 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{276 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{277 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{278 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{279 \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, given a filename (or an open file or memory block-\/-\/see header}}
\DoxyCodeLine{280 \textcolor{comment}{// file for details) containing image data, you can query for the "{}most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{281 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriate"{} interface to use (that is, whether the image is HDR or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{282 \textcolor{comment}{// not), using:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{283 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{284 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_is\_hdr(char *filename);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{285 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{286 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{287 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{288 \textcolor{comment}{// iPhone PNG support:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{289 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{290 \textcolor{comment}{// We optionally support converting iPhone-\/formatted PNGs (which store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{291 \textcolor{comment}{// premultiplied BGRA) back to RGB, even though they're internally encoded}}
\DoxyCodeLine{292 \textcolor{comment}{// differently. To enable this conversion, call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{293 \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_convert\_iphone\_png\_to\_rgb(1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{294 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{295 \textcolor{comment}{// Call stbi\_set\_unpremultiply\_on\_load(1) as well to force a divide per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{296 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel to remove any premultiplied alpha *only* if the image file explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{297 \textcolor{comment}{// says there's premultiplied data (currently only happens in iPhone images,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{298 \textcolor{comment}{// and only if iPhone convert-\/to-\/rgb processing is on).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{299 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{300 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{301 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{302 \textcolor{comment}{// ADDITIONAL CONFIGURATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{303 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{304 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ You can suppress implementation of any of the decoders to reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{305 \textcolor{comment}{//    your code footprint by \#defining one or more of the following}}
\DoxyCodeLine{306 \textcolor{comment}{//    symbols before creating the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{307 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{308 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{309 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{310 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{311 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{312 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_TGA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{313 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_GIF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{314 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_HDR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{315 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_PIC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{316 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_PNM   (.ppm and .pgm)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{317 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{318 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ You can request *only* certain decoders and suppress all other ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{319 \textcolor{comment}{//    (this will be more forward-\/compatible, as addition of new decoders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{320 \textcolor{comment}{//    doesn't require you to disable them explicitly):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{321 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{322 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{323 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{324 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{325 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{326 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_TGA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{327 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_GIF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{328 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_HDR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{329 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_PIC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{330 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_PNM   (.ppm and .pgm)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{331 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{332 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ If you use STBI\_NO\_PNG (or \_ONLY\_ without PNG), and you still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{333 \textcolor{comment}{//     want the zlib decoder to be available, \#define STBI\_SUPPORT\_ZLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{334 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{335 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ If you define STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS, stb\_image will reject images greater}}
\DoxyCodeLine{336 \textcolor{comment}{//    than that size (in either width or height) without further processing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{337 \textcolor{comment}{//    This is to let programs in the wild set an upper bound to prevent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{338 \textcolor{comment}{//    denial-\/of-\/service attacks on untrusted data, as one could generate a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{339 \textcolor{comment}{//    valid image of gigantic dimensions and force stb\_image to allocate a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{340 \textcolor{comment}{//    huge block of memory and spend disproportionate time decoding it. By}}
\DoxyCodeLine{341 \textcolor{comment}{//    default this is set to (1 << 24), which is 16777216, but that's still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{342 \textcolor{comment}{//    very big.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{343 }
\DoxyCodeLine{344 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_STDIO}}

\DoxyCodeLine{672 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_\_GNUC\_\_) \&\& defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET) \&\& !defined(\_\_SSE2\_\_) \&\& !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{673 \textcolor{comment}{// gcc doesn't support sse2 intrinsics unless you compile with -\/msse2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{674 \textcolor{comment}{// which in turn means it gets to use SSE2 everywhere. This is unfortunate,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{675 \textcolor{comment}{// but previous attempts to provide the SSE2 functions with runtime}}
\DoxyCodeLine{676 \textcolor{comment}{// detection caused numerous issues. The way architecture extensions are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{677 \textcolor{comment}{// exposed in GCC/Clang is, sadly, not really suited for one-\/file libs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{678 \textcolor{comment}{// New behavior: if compiled with -\/msse2, we use SSE2 without any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{679 \textcolor{comment}{// detection; if not, we don't use it at all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{680 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{681 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{682 }
\DoxyCodeLine{683 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_\_MINGW32\_\_) \&\& defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET) \&\& !defined(STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2) \&\& !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{684 \textcolor{comment}{// Note that \_\_MINGW32\_\_ doesn't actually mean 32-\/bit, so we have to avoid STBI\_\_X64\_TARGET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{685 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{686 \textcolor{comment}{// 32-\/bit MinGW wants ESP to be 16-\/byte aligned, but this is not in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{687 \textcolor{comment}{// Windows ABI and VC++ as well as Windows DLLs don't maintain that invariant.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{688 \textcolor{comment}{// As a result, enabling SSE2 on 32-\/bit MinGW is dangerous when not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{689 \textcolor{comment}{// simultaneously enabling "{}-\/mstackrealign"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{690 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{691 \textcolor{comment}{// See https://github.com/nothings/stb/issues/81 for more information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{692 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{693 \textcolor{comment}{// So default to no SSE2 on 32-\/bit MinGW. If you've read this far and added}}
\DoxyCodeLine{694 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/mstackrealign to your build settings, feel free to \#define STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{695 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{696 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{697 }

\DoxyCodeLine{959 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* stbi\_\_malloc(\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} size)}
\DoxyCodeLine{960 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{961     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} STBI\_MALLOC(size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{962 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{963 }
\DoxyCodeLine{964 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image uses ints pervasively, including for offset calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{965 \textcolor{comment}{// therefore the largest decoded image size we can support with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{966 \textcolor{comment}{// current code, even on 64-\/bit targets, is INT\_MAX. this is not a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{967 \textcolor{comment}{// significant limitation for the intended use case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{968 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{969 \textcolor{comment}{// we do, however, need to make sure our size calculations don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{970 \textcolor{comment}{// overflow. hence a few helper functions for size calculations that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{971 \textcolor{comment}{// multiply integers together, making sure that they're non-\/negative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{972 \textcolor{comment}{// and no overflow occurs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{973 }
\DoxyCodeLine{974 \textcolor{comment}{// return 1 if the sum is valid, 0 on overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{975 \textcolor{comment}{// negative terms are considered invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{976 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_addsizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{977 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{978     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{979     \textcolor{comment}{// now 0 <= b <= INT\_MAX, hence also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{980     \textcolor{comment}{// 0 <= INT\_MAX -\/ b <= INTMAX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{981     \textcolor{comment}{// And "{}a + b <= INT\_MAX"{} (which might overflow) is the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{982     \textcolor{comment}{// same as a <= INT\_MAX -\/ b (no overflow)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{983     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a <= INT\_MAX -\/ b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{984 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{985 }
\DoxyCodeLine{986 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1 if the product is valid, 0 on overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{987 \textcolor{comment}{// negative factors are considered invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{988 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{989 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{990     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (a < 0 || b < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{991     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b == 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1; \textcolor{comment}{// mul-\/by-\/0 is always safe}}
\DoxyCodeLine{992     \textcolor{comment}{// portable way to check for no overflows in a*b}}
\DoxyCodeLine{993     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a <= INT\_MAX / b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{994 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{995 }
\DoxyCodeLine{996 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if !defined(STBI\_NO\_JPEG) || !defined(STBI\_NO\_PNG) || !defined(STBI\_NO\_TGA) || !defined(STBI\_NO\_HDR)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{997 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1 if "{}a*b + add"{} has no negative terms/factors and doesn't overflow}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1179 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_vertical\_flip(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* image, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} h, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bytes\_per\_pixel)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1180 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1181     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} row;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1182     \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} bytes\_per\_row = (size\_t)w * bytes\_per\_pixel;}

\DoxyCodeLine{1184     stbi\_uc* bytes = (stbi\_uc*)image;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1185 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1186     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (row = 0; row < (h >> 1); row++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1187         stbi\_uc* row0 = bytes + row * bytes\_per\_row;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1188         stbi\_uc* row1 = bytes + (h -\/ row -\/ 1) * bytes\_per\_row;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1189         \textcolor{comment}{// swap row0 with row1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1190         \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} bytes\_left = bytes\_per\_row;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1191         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (bytes\_left) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1192             \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} bytes\_copy = (bytes\_left < \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(temp)) ? bytes\_left : \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(temp);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1193             memcpy(temp, row0, bytes\_copy);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1194             memcpy(row0, row1, bytes\_copy);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1195             memcpy(row1, temp, bytes\_copy);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1196             row0 += bytes\_copy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1197             row1 += bytes\_copy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1198             bytes\_left -\/= bytes\_copy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1199         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1200     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1875 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1876 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't support delayed output of y-\/dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1877 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ simple interface (only one output format: 8-\/bit interleaved RGB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1878 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't try to recover corrupt jpegs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1879 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't allow partial loading, loading multiple at once}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1880 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ still fast on x86 (copying globals into locals doesn't help x86)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1881 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ allocates lots of intermediate memory (full size of all components)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1882 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ non-\/interleaved case requires this anyway}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1883 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ allows good upsampling (see next)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1884 \textcolor{comment}{//    high-\/quality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1885 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ upsampled channels are bilinearly interpolated, even across blocks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1886 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ quality integer IDCT derived from IJG's 'slow'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1887 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1888 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman; reasonable integer IDCT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1889 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ some SIMD kernels for common paths on targets with SSE2/NEON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1890 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ uses a lot of intermediate memory, could cache poorly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1891 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1892 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1893 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1962 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_build\_huffman(stbi\_\_huffman* h, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* count)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1963 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1964     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j, k = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1965     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1966     \textcolor{comment}{// build size list for each symbol (from JPEG spec)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1967     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < 16; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1968         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < count[i]; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1969             h-\/>size[k++] = (stbi\_uc)(i + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1970     h-\/>size[k] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1971 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1972     \textcolor{comment}{// compute actual symbols (from jpeg spec)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1973     code = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1974     k = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1975     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 1; j <= 16; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1976         \textcolor{comment}{// compute delta to add to code to compute symbol id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1977         h-\/>delta[j] = k -\/ code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1978         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (h-\/>size[k] == j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1979             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (h-\/>size[k] == j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1980                 h-\/>code[k++] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(code++);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1981             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code -\/ 1 >= (1u << j)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad code lengths"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt JPEG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1982         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1983         \textcolor{comment}{// compute largest code + 1 for this size, preshifted as needed later}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1984         h-\/>maxcode[j] = code << (16 -\/ j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1985         code <<= 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1986     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1987     h-\/>maxcode[j] = 0xffffffff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1988 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1989     \textcolor{comment}{// build non-\/spec acceleration table; 255 is flag for not-\/accelerated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1990     memset(h-\/>fast, 255, 1 << FAST\_BITS);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1991     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < k; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1992         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = h-\/>size[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1993         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s <= FAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1994             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c = h-\/>code[i] << (FAST\_BITS -\/ s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1995             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = 1 << (FAST\_BITS -\/ s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1996             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < m; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1997                 h-\/>fast[c + j] = (stbi\_uc)i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1998             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1999         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2000     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2001     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2002 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2003 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2004 \textcolor{comment}{// build a table that decodes both magnitude and value of small ACs in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2005 \textcolor{comment}{// one go.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2006 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_build\_fast\_ac(stbi\_\_int16* fast\_ac, stbi\_\_huffman* h)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2007 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2008     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2009     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < (1 << FAST\_BITS); ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2010         stbi\_uc fast = h-\/>fast[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2011         fast\_ac[i] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2012         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fast < 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2013             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rs = h-\/>values[fast];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2014             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} run = (rs >> 4) \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2015             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} magbits = rs \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2016             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} len = h-\/>size[fast];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2017 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2018             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (magbits \&\& len + magbits <= FAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2019                 \textcolor{comment}{// magnitude code followed by receive\_extend code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2020                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} k = ((i << len) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1)) >> (FAST\_BITS -\/ magbits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2021                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = 1 << (magbits -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2022                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k < m) k += (\string~0U << magbits) + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2023                 \textcolor{comment}{// if the result is small enough, we can fit it in fast\_ac table}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2024                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k >= -\/128 \&\& k <= 127)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2025                     fast\_ac[i] = (stbi\_\_int16)((k * 256) + (run * 16) + (len + magbits));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2026             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2027         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2028     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2029 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2030 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2031 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(stbi\_\_jpeg* j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2032 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2033     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2034         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b = j-\/>nomore ? 0 : stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2035         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b == 0xff) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2036             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2037             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (c == 0xff) c = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s); \textcolor{comment}{// consume fill bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2038             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c != 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2039                 j-\/>marker = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2040                 j-\/>nomore = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2041                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2042             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2043         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2044         j-\/>code\_buffer |= b << (24 -\/ j-\/>code\_bits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2045         j-\/>code\_bits += 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2046     \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (j-\/>code\_bits <= 24);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2047 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2048 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2049 \textcolor{comment}{// (1 << n) -\/ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2050 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_\_uint32 stbi\_\_bmask[17] = \{ 0,1,3,7,15,31,63,127,255,511,1023,2047,4095,8191,16383,32767,65535 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2051 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2052 \textcolor{comment}{// decode a jpeg huffman value from the bitstream}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2053 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_jpeg\_huff\_decode(stbi\_\_jpeg* j, stbi\_\_huffman* h)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2054 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2055     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2056     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c, k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2057 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2058     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>code\_bits < 16) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2059 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2060     \textcolor{comment}{// look at the top FAST\_BITS and determine what symbol ID it is,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2061     \textcolor{comment}{// if the code is <= FAST\_BITS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2062     c = (j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ FAST\_BITS)) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2063     k = h-\/>fast[c];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2064     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k < 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2065         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = h-\/>size[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2066         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s > j-\/>code\_bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2067             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2068         j-\/>code\_buffer <<= s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2069         j-\/>code\_bits -\/= s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2070         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} h-\/>values[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2071     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2072 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2073     \textcolor{comment}{// naive test is to shift the code\_buffer down so k bits are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2074     \textcolor{comment}{// valid, then test against maxcode. To speed this up, we've}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2075     \textcolor{comment}{// preshifted maxcode left so that it has (16-\/k) 0s at the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2076     \textcolor{comment}{// end; in other words, regardless of the number of bits, it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2077     \textcolor{comment}{// wants to be compared against something shifted to have 16;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2078     \textcolor{comment}{// that way we don't need to shift inside the loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2079     temp = j-\/>code\_buffer >> 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2080     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k = FAST\_BITS + 1; ; ++k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2081         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (temp < h-\/>maxcode[k])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2082             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2083     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k == 17) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2084         \textcolor{comment}{// error! code not found}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2085         j-\/>code\_bits -\/= 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2086         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2087     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2088 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2089     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k > j-\/>code\_bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2090         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2091 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2092     \textcolor{comment}{// convert the huffman code to the symbol id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2093     c = ((j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ k)) \& stbi\_\_bmask[k]) + h-\/>delta[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2094     STBI\_ASSERT((((j-\/>code\_buffer) >> (32 -\/ h-\/>size[c])) \& stbi\_\_bmask[h-\/>size[c]]) == h-\/>code[c]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2095 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2096     \textcolor{comment}{// convert the id to a symbol}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2097     j-\/>code\_bits -\/= k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2098     j-\/>code\_buffer <<= k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2099     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} h-\/>values[c];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2100 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2101 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2102 \textcolor{comment}{// bias[n] = (-\/1<<n) + 1}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2169 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2170     \textcolor{comment}{// 0 all the ac values now so we can do it 32-\/bits at a time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2171     memset(data, 0, 64 * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(data[0]));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2172 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2173     diff = t ? stbi\_\_extend\_receive(j, t) : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2174     dc = j-\/>img\_comp[b].dc\_pred + diff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2175     j-\/>img\_comp[b].dc\_pred = dc;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2176     data[0] = (short)(dc * dequant[0]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2177 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2178     \textcolor{comment}{// decode AC components, see JPEG spec}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2179     k = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2180     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2181         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} zig;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2182         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c, r, s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2183         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>code\_bits < 16) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2184         c = (j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ FAST\_BITS)) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2185         r = fac[c];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2186         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// fast-\/AC path}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2187             k += (r >> 4) \& 15; \textcolor{comment}{// run}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2188             s = r \& 15; \textcolor{comment}{// combined length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2189             j-\/>code\_buffer <<= s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2190             j-\/>code\_bits -\/= s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2191             \textcolor{comment}{// decode into unzigzag'd location}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2192             zig = stbi\_\_jpeg\_dezigzag[k++];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2193             data[zig] = (short)((r >> 8) * dequant[zig]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2194         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2195         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2196             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rs = stbi\_\_jpeg\_huff\_decode(j, hac);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2197             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rs < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad huffman code"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt JPEG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{2198             s = rs \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2199             r = rs >> 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2200             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2201                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rs != 0xf0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break}; \textcolor{comment}{// end block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2202                 k += 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2203             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2204             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2205                 k += r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2206                 \textcolor{comment}{// decode into unzigzag'd location}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2207                 zig = stbi\_\_jpeg\_dezigzag[k++];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2208                 data[zig] = (short)(stbi\_\_extend\_receive(j, s) * dequant[zig]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2209             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2210         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2211     \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (k < 64);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2212     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2213 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2422 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_idct\_block(stbi\_uc* out, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_stride, \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} data[64])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2423 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2424     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, val[64], * v = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2425     stbi\_uc* o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2426     \textcolor{keywordtype}{short}* d = data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2427 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2428     \textcolor{comment}{// columns}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2429     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < 8; ++i, ++d, ++v) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2430         \textcolor{comment}{// if all zeroes, shortcut -\/-\/ this avoids dequantizing 0s and IDCTing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2431         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (d[8] == 0 \&\& d[16] == 0 \&\& d[24] == 0 \&\& d[32] == 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{2432             \&\& d[40] == 0 \&\& d[48] == 0 \&\& d[56] == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2433             \textcolor{comment}{//    no shortcut                 0     seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2434             \textcolor{comment}{//    (1|2|3|4|5|6|7)==0          0     seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2435             \textcolor{comment}{//    all separate               -\/0.047 seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2436             \textcolor{comment}{//    1 \&\& 2|3 \&\& 4|5 \&\& 6|7:    -\/0.047 seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2437             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} dcterm = d[0] * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2438             v[0] = v[8] = v[16] = v[24] = v[32] = v[40] = v[48] = v[56] = dcterm;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2439         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2440         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2441             STBI\_\_IDCT\_1D(d[0], d[8], d[16], d[24], d[32], d[40], d[48], d[56])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2442                 \textcolor{comment}{// constants scaled things up by 1<<12; let's bring them back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2443                 \textcolor{comment}{// down, but keep 2 extra bits of precision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2444                 x0 += 512; x1 += 512; x2 += 512; x3 += 512;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2445             v[0] = (x0 + t3) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2446             v[56] = (x0 -\/ t3) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2447             v[8] = (x1 + t2) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2448             v[48] = (x1 -\/ t2) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2449             v[16] = (x2 + t1) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2450             v[40] = (x2 -\/ t1) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2451             v[24] = (x3 + t0) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2452             v[32] = (x3 -\/ t0) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2453         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2454     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2455 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2456     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0, v = val, o = out; i < 8; ++i, v += 8, o += out\_stride) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2457         \textcolor{comment}{// no fast case since the first 1D IDCT spread components out}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2458         STBI\_\_IDCT\_1D(v[0], v[1], v[2], v[3], v[4], v[5], v[6], v[7])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2459             \textcolor{comment}{// constants scaled things up by 1<<12, plus we had 1<<2 from first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2460             \textcolor{comment}{// loop, plus horizontal and vertical each scale by sqrt(8) so together}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2461             \textcolor{comment}{// we've got an extra 1<<3, so 1<<17 total we need to remove.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2462             \textcolor{comment}{// so we want to round that, which means adding 0.5 * 1<<17,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2463             \textcolor{comment}{// aka 65536. Also, we'll end up with -\/128 to 127 that we want}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2464             \textcolor{comment}{// to encode as 0..255 by adding 128, so we'll add that before the shift}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2465             x0 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2466         x1 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2467         x2 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2468         x3 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2469         \textcolor{comment}{// tried computing the shifts into temps, or'ing the temps to see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2470         \textcolor{comment}{// if any were out of range, but that was slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2471         o[0] = stbi\_\_clamp((x0 + t3) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2472         o[7] = stbi\_\_clamp((x0 -\/ t3) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2473         o[1] = stbi\_\_clamp((x1 + t2) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2474         o[6] = stbi\_\_clamp((x1 -\/ t2) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2475         o[2] = stbi\_\_clamp((x2 + t1) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2476         o[5] = stbi\_\_clamp((x2 -\/ t1) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2477         o[3] = stbi\_\_clamp((x3 + t0) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2478         o[4] = stbi\_\_clamp((x3 -\/ t0) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2479     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2480 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2481 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2482 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_SSE2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2483 \textcolor{comment}{// sse2 integer IDCT. not the fastest possible implementation but it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2484 \textcolor{comment}{// produces bit-\/identical results to the generic C version so it's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2485 \textcolor{comment}{// fully "{}transparent"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2486 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_idct\_simd(stbi\_uc* out, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_stride, \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} data[64])}

\DoxyCodeLine{2492     \textcolor{comment}{// dot product constant: even elems=x, odd elems=y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2493 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define dct\_const(x,y)  \_mm\_setr\_epi16((x),(y),(x),(y),(x),(y),(x),(y))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2494 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2495 \textcolor{comment}{// out(0) = c0[even]*x + c0[odd]*y   (c0, x, y 16-\/bit, out 32-\/bit)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2496 \textcolor{comment}{// out(1) = c1[even]*x + c1[odd]*y}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2498 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i c0\#\#lo = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16((x),(y)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2499 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i c0\#\#hi = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16((x),(y)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2500 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out0\#\#\_l = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#lo, c0); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2501 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out0\#\#\_h = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#hi, c0); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2502 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out1\#\#\_l = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#lo, c1); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2503 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out1\#\#\_h = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#hi, c1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2504 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2505    \textcolor{comment}{// out = in << 12  (in 16-\/bit, out 32-\/bit)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2506 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define dct\_widen(out, in) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2507 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out\#\#\_l = \_mm\_srai\_epi32(\_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), (in)), 4); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2508 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out\#\#\_h = \_mm\_srai\_epi32(\_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), (in)), 4)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2509 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2510    \textcolor{comment}{// wide add}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2522 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \{ \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2871 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_MARKER\_none  0xff}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2872 \textcolor{comment}{// if there's a pending marker from the entropy stream, return that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2873 \textcolor{comment}{// otherwise, fetch from the stream and get a marker. if there's no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2874 \textcolor{comment}{// marker, return 0xff, which is never a valid marker value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2875 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc stbi\_\_get\_marker(stbi\_\_jpeg* j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2876 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2877     stbi\_uc x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2878     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>marker != STBI\_\_MARKER\_none) \{ x = j-\/>marker; j-\/>marker = STBI\_\_MARKER\_none; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} x; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2879     x = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2880     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x != 0xff) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} STBI\_\_MARKER\_none;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2881     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (x == 0xff)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2882         x = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s); \textcolor{comment}{// consume repeated 0xff fill bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2883     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2884 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2885 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2886 \textcolor{comment}{// in each scan, we'll have scan\_n components, and the order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2887 \textcolor{comment}{// of the components is specified by order[]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2888 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_RESTART(x)     ((x) >= 0xd0 \&\& (x) <= 0xd7)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2889 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2890 \textcolor{comment}{// after a restart interval, stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset the entropy decoder and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2891 \textcolor{comment}{// the dc prediction}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2892 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset(stbi\_\_jpeg* j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2893 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2894     j-\/>code\_bits = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2895     j-\/>code\_buffer = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2896     j-\/>nomore = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2897     j-\/>img\_comp[0].dc\_pred = j-\/>img\_comp[1].dc\_pred = j-\/>img\_comp[2].dc\_pred = j-\/>img\_comp[3].dc\_pred = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2898     j-\/>marker = STBI\_\_MARKER\_none;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2899     j-\/>todo = j-\/>restart\_interval ? j-\/>restart\_interval : 0x7fffffff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2900     j-\/>eob\_run = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2901     \textcolor{comment}{// no more than 1<<31 MCUs if no restart\_interal? that's plenty safe,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2902     \textcolor{comment}{// since we don't even allow 1<<30 pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2903 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2904 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2905 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_parse\_entropy\_coded\_data(stbi\_\_jpeg* z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2906 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2907     stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2908     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!z-\/>progressive) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2909         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>scan\_n == 1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2910             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2911             STBI\_SIMD\_ALIGN(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}, data[64]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2912             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n = z-\/>order[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2913             \textcolor{comment}{// non-\/interleaved data, we just need to process one block at a time,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2914             \textcolor{comment}{// in trivial scanline order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2915             \textcolor{comment}{// number of blocks to do just depends on how many actual "{}pixels"{} this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2916             \textcolor{comment}{// component has, independent of interleaved MCU blocking and such}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2917             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w = (z-\/>img\_comp[n].x + 7) >> 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2918             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} h = (z-\/>img\_comp[n].y + 7) >> 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2919             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < h; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2920                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2921                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} ha = z-\/>img\_comp[n].ha;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2922                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_jpeg\_decode\_block(z, data, z-\/>huff\_dc + z-\/>img\_comp[n].hd, z-\/>huff\_ac + ha, z-\/>fast\_ac[ha], n, z-\/>dequant[z-\/>img\_comp[n].tq])) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2923                     z-\/>idct\_block\_kernel(z-\/>img\_comp[n].data + z-\/>img\_comp[n].w2 * j * 8 + i * 8, z-\/>img\_comp[n].w2, data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2924                     \textcolor{comment}{// every data block is an MCU, so countdown the restart interval}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2925                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (-\/-\/z-\/>todo <= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2926                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>code\_bits < 24) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2927                         \textcolor{comment}{// if it's NOT a restart, then just bail, so we get corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2928                         \textcolor{comment}{// rather than no data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2929                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!STBI\_\_RESTART(z-\/>marker)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2930                         stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2931                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2932                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2933             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2934             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2935         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2936         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{ \textcolor{comment}{// interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2937             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j, k, x, y;}
