\DoxyCodeLine{3432     out[0] = input[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3433     out[1] = stbi\_\_div4(input[0] * 3 + input[1] + 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3434     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 1; i < w -\/ 1; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3435         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n = 3 * input[i] + 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3436         out[i * 2 + 0] = stbi\_\_div4(n + input[i -\/ 1]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3437         out[i * 2 + 1] = stbi\_\_div4(n + input[i + 1]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3438     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3439     out[i * 2 + 0] = stbi\_\_div4(input[w -\/ 2] * 3 + input[w -\/ 1] + 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3440     out[i * 2 + 1] = input[w -\/ 1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3441 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3442     STBI\_NOTUSED(in\_far);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3443     STBI\_NOTUSED(hs);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3444 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3445     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3446 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3447 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3448 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define stbi\_\_div16(x) ((stbi\_uc) ((x) >> 4))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3449 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3450 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc* stbi\_\_resample\_row\_hv\_2(stbi\_uc* out, stbi\_uc* in\_near, stbi\_uc* in\_far, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} hs)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3451 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3452     \textcolor{comment}{// need to generate 2x2 samples for every one in input}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3453     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, t0, t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3454     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (w == 1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3455         out[0] = out[1] = stbi\_\_div4(3 * in\_near[0] + in\_far[0] + 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3456         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3457     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3458 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3459     t1 = 3 * in\_near[0] + in\_far[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3460     out[0] = stbi\_\_div4(t1 + 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3461     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 1; i < w; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3462         t0 = t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3463         t1 = 3 * in\_near[i] + in\_far[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3464         out[i * 2 -\/ 1] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t0 + t1 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3465         out[i * 2] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t1 + t0 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3466     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3467     out[w * 2 -\/ 1] = stbi\_\_div4(t1 + 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3468 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3469     STBI\_NOTUSED(hs);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3470 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3471     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3472 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3473 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3474 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_SSE2) || defined(STBI\_NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3475 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc* stbi\_\_resample\_row\_hv\_2\_simd(stbi\_uc* out, stbi\_uc* in\_near, stbi\_uc* in\_far, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} hs)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3476 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3477     \textcolor{comment}{// need to generate 2x2 samples for every one in input}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3478     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0, t0, t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3479 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3480     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (w == 1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3481         out[0] = out[1] = stbi\_\_div4(3 * in\_near[0] + in\_far[0] + 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3482         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3483     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3484 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3485     t1 = 3 * in\_near[0] + in\_far[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3486     \textcolor{comment}{// process groups of 8 pixels for as long as we can.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3487     \textcolor{comment}{// note we can't handle the last pixel in a row in this loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3488     \textcolor{comment}{// because we need to handle the filter boundary conditions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3489     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i < ((w -\/ 1) \& \string~7); i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3490 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_SSE2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3491         \textcolor{comment}{// load and perform the vertical filtering pass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3492         \textcolor{comment}{// this uses 3*x + y = 4*x + (y -\/ x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3493         \_\_m128i zero = \_mm\_setzero\_si128();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3494         \_\_m128i farb = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (in\_far + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3495         \_\_m128i nearb = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (in\_near + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3496         \_\_m128i farw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(farb, zero);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3497         \_\_m128i nearw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(nearb, zero);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498         \_\_m128i diff = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(farw, nearw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3499         \_\_m128i nears = \_mm\_slli\_epi16(nearw, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500         \_\_m128i curr = \_mm\_add\_epi16(nears, diff); \textcolor{comment}{// current row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3502         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter works the same based on shifted vers of current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503         \textcolor{comment}{// row. "{}prev"{} is current row shifted right by 1 pixel; we need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504         \textcolor{comment}{// insert the previous pixel value (from t1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3505         \textcolor{comment}{// "{}next"{} is current row shifted left by 1 pixel, with first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3506         \textcolor{comment}{// of next block of 8 pixels added in.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507         \_\_m128i prv0 = \_mm\_slli\_si128(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508         \_\_m128i nxt0 = \_mm\_srli\_si128(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3509         \_\_m128i prev = \_mm\_insert\_epi16(prv0, t1, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3510         \_\_m128i next = \_mm\_insert\_epi16(nxt0, 3 * in\_near[i + 8] + in\_far[i + 8], 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3511 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3512         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter, polyphase implementation since it's convenient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3513         \textcolor{comment}{// even pixels = 3*cur + prev = cur*4 + (prev -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3514         \textcolor{comment}{// odd  pixels = 3*cur + next = cur*4 + (next -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3515         \textcolor{comment}{// note the shared term.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3516         \_\_m128i bias = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3517         \_\_m128i curs = \_mm\_slli\_epi16(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3518         \_\_m128i prvd = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(prev, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3519         \_\_m128i nxtd = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(next, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3520         \_\_m128i curb = \_mm\_add\_epi16(curs, bias);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3521         \_\_m128i even = \_mm\_add\_epi16(prvd, curb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3522         \_\_m128i odd = \_mm\_add\_epi16(nxtd, curb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3523 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3524         \textcolor{comment}{// interleave even and odd pixels, then undo scaling.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3525         \_\_m128i int0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(even, odd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3526         \_\_m128i int1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(even, odd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3527         \_\_m128i de0 = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(int0, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3528         \_\_m128i de1 = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(int1, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3529 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3530         \textcolor{comment}{// pack and write output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3531         \_\_m128i outv = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(de0, de1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3532         \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i*) (out + i * 2), outv);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3533 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif defined(STBI\_NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3534         \textcolor{comment}{// load and perform the vertical filtering pass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3535         \textcolor{comment}{// this uses 3*x + y = 4*x + (y -\/ x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3536         uint8x8\_t farb = vld1\_u8(in\_far + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3537         uint8x8\_t nearb = vld1\_u8(in\_near + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3538         int16x8\_t diff = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vsubl\_u8(farb, nearb));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3539         int16x8\_t nears = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vshll\_n\_u8(nearb, 2));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3540         int16x8\_t curr = vaddq\_s16(nears, diff); \textcolor{comment}{// current row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3541 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3542         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter works the same based on shifted vers of current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3543         \textcolor{comment}{// row. "{}prev"{} is current row shifted right by 1 pixel; we need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3544         \textcolor{comment}{// insert the previous pixel value (from t1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3545         \textcolor{comment}{// "{}next"{} is current row shifted left by 1 pixel, with first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3546         \textcolor{comment}{// of next block of 8 pixels added in.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3547         int16x8\_t prv0 = vextq\_s16(curr, curr, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3548         int16x8\_t nxt0 = vextq\_s16(curr, curr, 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3549         int16x8\_t prev = vsetq\_lane\_s16(t1, prv0, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3550         int16x8\_t next = vsetq\_lane\_s16(3 * in\_near[i + 8] + in\_far[i + 8], nxt0, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3551 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3552         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter, polyphase implementation since it's convenient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3553         \textcolor{comment}{// even pixels = 3*cur + prev = cur*4 + (prev -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3554         \textcolor{comment}{// odd  pixels = 3*cur + next = cur*4 + (next -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3555         \textcolor{comment}{// note the shared term.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3556         int16x8\_t curs = vshlq\_n\_s16(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3557         int16x8\_t prvd = vsubq\_s16(prev, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3558         int16x8\_t nxtd = vsubq\_s16(next, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3559         int16x8\_t even = vaddq\_s16(curs, prvd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3560         int16x8\_t odd = vaddq\_s16(curs, nxtd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3561 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3562         \textcolor{comment}{// undo scaling and round, then store with even/odd phases interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3563         uint8x8x2\_t o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3564         o.val[0] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(even, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3565         o.val[1] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(odd, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3566         vst2\_u8(out + i * 2, o);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3567 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3568 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3569         \textcolor{comment}{// "{}previous"{} value for next iter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3570         t1 = 3 * in\_near[i + 7] + in\_far[i + 7];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3571     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3572 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3573     t0 = t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3574     t1 = 3 * in\_near[i] + in\_far[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3575     out[i * 2] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t1 + t0 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3576 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3577     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (++i; i < w; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3578         t0 = t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3579         t1 = 3 * in\_near[i] + in\_far[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3580         out[i * 2 -\/ 1] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t0 + t1 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3581         out[i * 2] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t1 + t0 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3582     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3583     out[w * 2 -\/ 1] = stbi\_\_div4(t1 + 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3584 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3585     STBI\_NOTUSED(hs);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3586 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3587     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3588 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3589 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3590 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3591 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc* stbi\_\_resample\_row\_generic(stbi\_uc* out, stbi\_uc* in\_near, stbi\_uc* in\_far, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} hs)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3592 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3593     \textcolor{comment}{// resample with nearest-\/neighbor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3594     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3595     STBI\_NOTUSED(in\_far);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3596     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3597         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < hs; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3598             out[i * hs + j] = in\_near[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3599     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3600 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3601 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3602 \textcolor{comment}{// this is a reduced-\/precision calculation of YCbCr-\/to-\/RGB introduced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3603 \textcolor{comment}{// to make sure the code produces the same results in both SIMD and scalar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3604 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define stbi\_\_float2fixed(x)  (((int) ((x) * 4096.0f + 0.5f)) << 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3605 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_row(stbi\_uc* out, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc* y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc* pcb, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc* pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3606 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3607     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3608     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < count; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3609         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y\_fixed = (y[i] << 20) + (1 << 19); \textcolor{comment}{// rounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3610         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r, g, b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3611         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cr = pcr[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3612         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cb = pcb[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3613         r = y\_fixed + cr * stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.40200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3614         g = y\_fixed + (cr * -\/stbi\_\_float2fixed(0.71414f)) + ((cb * -\/stbi\_\_float2fixed(0.34414f)) \& 0xffff0000);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3615         b = y\_fixed + cb * stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.77200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3616         r >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3617         g >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3618         b >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3619         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})r > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r < 0) r = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} r = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3620         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})g > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g < 0) g = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} g = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3621         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})b > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) b = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} b = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3622         out[0] = (stbi\_uc)r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3623         out[1] = (stbi\_uc)g;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3624         out[2] = (stbi\_uc)b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3625         out[3] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3626         out += step;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3627     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3628 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3629 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3630 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_SSE2) || defined(STBI\_NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3631 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_simd(stbi\_uc* out, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const}* y, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const}* pcb, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const}* pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3632 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3633     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3634 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3635 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_SSE2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3636     \textcolor{comment}{// step == 3 is pretty ugly on the final interleave, and i'm not convinced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3637     \textcolor{comment}{// it's useful in practice (you wouldn't use it for textures, for example).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3638     \textcolor{comment}{// so just accelerate step == 4 case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3639     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (step == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3640         \textcolor{comment}{// this is a fairly straightforward implementation and not super-\/optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3641         \_\_m128i signflip = \_mm\_set1\_epi8(-\/0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3642         \_\_m128i cr\_const0 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.40200f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3643         \_\_m128i cr\_const1 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.71414f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3644         \_\_m128i cb\_const0 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.34414f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3645         \_\_m128i cb\_const1 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.77200f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3646         \_\_m128i y\_bias = \_mm\_set1\_epi8((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char})(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char})128);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3647         \_\_m128i xw = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(255); \textcolor{comment}{// alpha channel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3648 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3649         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i + 7 < count; i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3650             \textcolor{comment}{// load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3651             \_\_m128i y\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (y + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3652             \_\_m128i cr\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (pcr + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3653             \_\_m128i cb\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (pcb + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3654             \_\_m128i cr\_biased = \_mm\_xor\_si128(cr\_bytes, signflip); \textcolor{comment}{// -\/128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3655             \_\_m128i cb\_biased = \_mm\_xor\_si128(cb\_bytes, signflip); \textcolor{comment}{// -\/128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3656 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3657             \textcolor{comment}{// unpack to short (and left-\/shift cr, cb by 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3658             \_\_m128i yw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(y\_bias, y\_bytes);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3659             \_\_m128i crw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), cr\_biased);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3660             \_\_m128i cbw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), cb\_biased);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3661 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3662             \textcolor{comment}{// color transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3663             \_\_m128i yws = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(yw, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3664             \_\_m128i cr0 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cr\_const0, crw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3665             \_\_m128i cb0 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cb\_const0, cbw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3666             \_\_m128i cb1 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cbw, cb\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3667             \_\_m128i cr1 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(crw, cr\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3668             \_\_m128i rws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(cr0, yws);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3669             \_\_m128i gwt = \_mm\_add\_epi16(cb0, yws);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3670             \_\_m128i bws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(yws, cb1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3671             \_\_m128i gws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(gwt, cr1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3672 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3673             \textcolor{comment}{// descale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3674             \_\_m128i rw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(rws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3675             \_\_m128i bw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(bws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3676             \_\_m128i gw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(gws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3677 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3678             \textcolor{comment}{// back to byte, set up for transpose}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3679             \_\_m128i brb = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(rw, bw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3680             \_\_m128i gxb = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(gw, xw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3681 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3682             \textcolor{comment}{// transpose to interleave channels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3683             \_\_m128i t0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(brb, gxb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3684             \_\_m128i t1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi8(brb, gxb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3685             \_\_m128i o0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(t0, t1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3686             \_\_m128i o1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(t0, t1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3687 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3688             \textcolor{comment}{// store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3689             \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i*) (out + 0), o0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3690             \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i*) (out + 16), o1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3691             out += 32;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3692         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3693     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3694 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3695 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3696 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_NEON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3697     \textcolor{comment}{// in this version, step=3 support would be easy to add. but is there demand?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3698     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (step == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3699         \textcolor{comment}{// this is a fairly straightforward implementation and not super-\/optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3700         uint8x8\_t signflip = vdup\_n\_u8(0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3701         int16x8\_t cr\_const0 = vdupq\_n\_s16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.40200f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3702         int16x8\_t cr\_const1 = vdupq\_n\_s16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.71414f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3703         int16x8\_t cb\_const0 = vdupq\_n\_s16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.34414f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3704         int16x8\_t cb\_const1 = vdupq\_n\_s16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.77200f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3705 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3706         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i + 7 < count; i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3707             \textcolor{comment}{// load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3708             uint8x8\_t y\_bytes = vld1\_u8(y + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3709             uint8x8\_t cr\_bytes = vld1\_u8(pcr + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3710             uint8x8\_t cb\_bytes = vld1\_u8(pcb + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3711             int8x8\_t cr\_biased = vreinterpret\_s8\_u8(vsub\_u8(cr\_bytes, signflip));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3712             int8x8\_t cb\_biased = vreinterpret\_s8\_u8(vsub\_u8(cb\_bytes, signflip));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3713 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3714             \textcolor{comment}{// expand to s16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3715             int16x8\_t yws = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vshll\_n\_u8(y\_bytes, 4));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3716             int16x8\_t crw = vshll\_n\_s8(cr\_biased, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3717             int16x8\_t cbw = vshll\_n\_s8(cb\_biased, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3718 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3719             \textcolor{comment}{// color transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3720             int16x8\_t cr0 = vqdmulhq\_s16(crw, cr\_const0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3721             int16x8\_t cb0 = vqdmulhq\_s16(cbw, cb\_const0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3722             int16x8\_t cr1 = vqdmulhq\_s16(crw, cr\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3723             int16x8\_t cb1 = vqdmulhq\_s16(cbw, cb\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3724             int16x8\_t rws = vaddq\_s16(yws, cr0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3725             int16x8\_t gws = vaddq\_s16(vaddq\_s16(yws, cb0), cr1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3726             int16x8\_t bws = vaddq\_s16(yws, cb1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3727 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3728             \textcolor{comment}{// undo scaling, round, convert to byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3729             uint8x8x4\_t o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3730             o.val[0] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(rws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3731             o.val[1] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(gws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3732             o.val[2] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(bws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3733             o.val[3] = vdup\_n\_u8(255);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3734 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3735             \textcolor{comment}{// store, interleaving r/g/b/a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3736             vst4\_u8(out, o);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3737             out += 8 * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3738         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3739     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3740 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3741 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3742     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i < count; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3743         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y\_fixed = (y[i] << 20) + (1 << 19); \textcolor{comment}{// rounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3744         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r, g, b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3745         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cr = pcr[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3746         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cb = pcb[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3747         r = y\_fixed + cr * stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.40200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3748         g = y\_fixed + cr * -\/stbi\_\_float2fixed(0.71414f) + ((cb * -\/stbi\_\_float2fixed(0.34414f)) \& 0xffff0000);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3749         b = y\_fixed + cb * stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.77200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3750         r >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3751         g >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3752         b >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3753         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})r > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r < 0) r = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} r = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3754         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})g > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g < 0) g = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} g = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3755         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})b > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) b = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} b = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3756         out[0] = (stbi\_uc)r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3757         out[1] = (stbi\_uc)g;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3758         out[2] = (stbi\_uc)b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3759         out[3] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3760         out += step;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3761     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3762 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3763 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4032 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain zlib decode    v0.2  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4033 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4034 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all input must be provided in an upfront buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4035 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all output is written to a single output buffer (can malloc/realloc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4036 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4037 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4038 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4039 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_ZLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4040 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4041 \textcolor{comment}{// fast-\/way is faster to check than jpeg huffman, but slow way is slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4042 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS  9 }\textcolor{comment}{// accelerate all cases in default tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4043 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZFAST\_MASK  ((1 << STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS) -\/ 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4044 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZNSYMS 288 }\textcolor{comment}{// number of symbols in literal/length alphabet}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4045 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4046 \textcolor{comment}{// zlib-\/style huffman encoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4047 \textcolor{comment}{// (jpegs packs from left, zlib from right, so can't share code)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4048 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4049 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4050     stbi\_\_uint16 fast[1 << STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS];}

\DoxyCodeLine{4058 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_bitreverse16(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4059 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4060     n = ((n \& 0xAAAA) >> 1) | ((n \& 0x5555) << 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4061     n = ((n \& 0xCCCC) >> 2) | ((n \& 0x3333) << 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4062     n = ((n \& 0xF0F0) >> 4) | ((n \& 0x0F0F) << 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4063     n = ((n \& 0xFF00) >> 8) | ((n \& 0x00FF) << 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4064     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4065 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4068 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4069     STBI\_ASSERT(bits <= 16);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4070     \textcolor{comment}{// to bit reverse n bits, reverse 16 and shift}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4086     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 1; i < 16; ++i)}

\DoxyCodeLine{4093         z-\/>firstsymbol[i] = (stbi\_\_uint16)k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4094         code = (code + sizes[i]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4095         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (sizes[i])}

\DoxyCodeLine{4097         z-\/>maxcode[i] = code << (16 -\/ i); \textcolor{comment}{// preshift for inner loop}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4099         k += sizes[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4100     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4103         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = sizelist[i];}

\DoxyCodeLine{4105             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c = next\_code[s] -\/ z-\/>firstcode[s] + z-\/>firstsymbol[s];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4106             stbi\_\_uint16 fastv = (stbi\_\_uint16)((s << 9) | i);}

\DoxyCodeLine{4108             z-\/>value[c] = (stbi\_\_uint16)i;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4113                     j += (1 << s);}

\DoxyCodeLine{4115             \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4117         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4118     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4119     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4174 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_zhuffman\_decode\_slowpath(stbi\_\_zbuf* a, stbi\_\_zhuffman* z)}

\DoxyCodeLine{4178     \textcolor{comment}{// use jpeg approach, which requires MSbits at top}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4536 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain "{}baseline"{} PNG decoder   v0.10  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4537 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4538 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ only 8-\/bit samples}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4539 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ no CRC checking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4540 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ allocates lots of intermediate memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4541 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ avoids problem of streaming data between subsystems}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4542 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ avoids explicit window management}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4543 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4544 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ uses stb\_zlib, a PD zlib implementation with fast huffman decoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4545 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4632 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4633     \textcolor{comment}{// we used to check for exact match between raw\_len and img\_len on non-\/interlaced PNGs,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4634     \textcolor{comment}{// but issue \#276 reported a PNG in the wild that had extra data at the end (all zeros),}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4637 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4639         stbi\_uc* cur = a-\/>out + stride * j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4640         stbi\_uc* prior;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4641         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} filter = *raw++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4642 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4643         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (filter > 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4644             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}invalid filter"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PNG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4645 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4646         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth < 8) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4648             cur += x * out\_n -\/ img\_width\_bytes; \textcolor{comment}{// store output to the rightmost img\_len bytes, so we can decode in place}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4649             filter\_bytes = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4650             width = img\_width\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4651         \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4653 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4654         \textcolor{comment}{// if first row, use special filter that doesn't sample previous row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4655         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j == 0) filter = first\_row\_filter[filter];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4656 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4657         \textcolor{comment}{// handle first byte explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4658         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k = 0; k < filter\_bytes; ++k) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4659             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (filter) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4660             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_none: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4661             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_sub: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4662             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_up: cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + prior[k]); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4663             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_avg: cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + (prior[k] >> 1)); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4664             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_paeth: cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + stbi\_\_paeth(0, prior[k], 0)); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4665             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_avg\_first: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4666             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_paeth\_first: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4667             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4668         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4669 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4670         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4671             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (img\_n != out\_n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4672                 cur[img\_n] = 255; \textcolor{comment}{// first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4673             raw += img\_n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4674             cur += out\_n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4675             prior += out\_n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4676         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4677         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4678             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (img\_n != out\_n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4679                 cur[filter\_bytes] = 255; \textcolor{comment}{// first pixel top byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4680                 cur[filter\_bytes + 1] = 255; \textcolor{comment}{// first pixel bottom byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4681             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4682             raw += filter\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4683             cur += output\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4684             prior += output\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4685         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4686         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4687             raw += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4688             cur += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4689             prior += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4690         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4691 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4692         \textcolor{comment}{// this is a little gross, so that we don't switch per-\/pixel or per-\/component}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4693         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth < 8 || img\_n == out\_n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4694             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} nk = (width -\/ 1) * filter\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4695 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_CASE(f) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4696 \textcolor{preprocessor}{             case f:     \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4697 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                for (k=0; k < nk; ++k)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4698             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (filter) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4699                 \textcolor{comment}{// "{}none"{} filter turns into a memcpy here; make that explicit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4700             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_none:         memcpy(cur, raw, nk); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4701                 STBI\_\_CASE(STBI\_\_F\_sub) \{ cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + cur[k -\/ filter\_bytes]); \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4702                 STBI\_\_CASE(STBI\_\_F\_up) \{ cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + prior[k]); \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4703                 STBI\_\_CASE(STBI\_\_F\_avg) \{ cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + ((prior[k] + cur[k -\/ filter\_bytes]) >> 1)); \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}

\DoxyCodeLine{4705                 STBI\_\_CASE(STBI\_\_F\_avg\_first) \{ cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + (cur[k -\/ filter\_bytes] >> 1)); \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4706                 STBI\_\_CASE(STBI\_\_F\_paeth\_first) \{ cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + stbi\_\_paeth(cur[k -\/ filter\_bytes], 0, 0)); \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4707             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4708 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#undef STBI\_\_CASE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4709             raw += nk;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4710         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4711         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4712             STBI\_ASSERT(img\_n + 1 == out\_n);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4713 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_CASE(f) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4714 \textcolor{preprocessor}{             case f:     \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4715 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                for (i=x-\/1; i >= 1; -\/-\/i, cur[filter\_bytes]=255,raw+=filter\_bytes,cur+=output\_bytes,prior+=output\_bytes) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4716 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                   for (k=0; k < filter\_bytes; ++k)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4717             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (filter) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4718                 STBI\_\_CASE(STBI\_\_F\_none) \{ cur[k] = raw[k]; \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4719                 STBI\_\_CASE(STBI\_\_F\_sub) \{ cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + cur[k -\/ output\_bytes]); \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}

\DoxyCodeLine{4726 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#undef STBI\_\_CASE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4727 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4728             \textcolor{comment}{// the loop above sets the high byte of the pixels' alpha, but for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4729             \textcolor{comment}{// 16 bit png files we also need the low byte set. we'll do that here.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4730             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4731                 cur = a-\/>out + stride * j; \textcolor{comment}{// start at the beginning of the row again}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4732                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < x; ++i, cur += output\_bytes) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4733                     cur[filter\_bytes + 1] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4734                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4735             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4736         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4737     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4738 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4739     \textcolor{comment}{// we make a separate pass to expand bits to pixels; for performance,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4740     \textcolor{comment}{// this could run two scanlines behind the above code, so it won't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4741     \textcolor{comment}{// intefere with filtering but will still be in the cache.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4742     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth < 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4743         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < y; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4744             stbi\_uc* cur = a-\/>out + stride * j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4745             stbi\_uc* in = a-\/>out + stride * j + x * out\_n -\/ img\_width\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4746             \textcolor{comment}{// unpack 1/2/4-\/bit into a 8-\/bit buffer. allows us to keep the common 8-\/bit path optimal at minimal cost for 1/2/4-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4747             \textcolor{comment}{// png guarante byte alignment, if width is not multiple of 8/4/2 we'll decode dummy trailing data that will be skipped in the later loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4748             stbi\_uc scale = (color == 0) ? stbi\_\_depth\_scale\_table[depth] : 1; \textcolor{comment}{// scale grayscale values to 0..255 range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4749 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4750             \textcolor{comment}{// note that the final byte might overshoot and write more data than desired.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4751             \textcolor{comment}{// we can allocate enough data that this never writes out of memory, but it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4752             \textcolor{comment}{// could also overwrite the next scanline. can it overwrite non-\/empty data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4753             \textcolor{comment}{// on the next scanline? yes, consider 1-\/pixel-\/wide scanlines with 1-\/bit-\/per-\/pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4754             \textcolor{comment}{// so we need to explicitly clamp the final ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4755 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4756             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4757                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k = x * img\_n; k >= 2; k -\/= 2, ++in) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4758                     *cur++ = scale * ((*in >> 4));}
\DoxyCodeLine{4759                     *cur++ = scale * ((*in) \& 0x0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4760                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4761                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k > 0) *cur++ = scale * ((*in >> 4));}
\DoxyCodeLine{4762             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4763             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 2) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4764                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k = x * img\_n; k >= 4; k -\/= 4, ++in) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4765                     *cur++ = scale * ((*in >> 6));}
\DoxyCodeLine{4766                     *cur++ = scale * ((*in >> 4) \& 0x03);}

\DoxyCodeLine{5354 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_bitcount(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5355 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5356     a = (a \& 0x55555555) + ((a >> 1) \& 0x55555555); \textcolor{comment}{// max 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5357     a = (a \& 0x33333333) + ((a >> 2) \& 0x33333333); \textcolor{comment}{// max 4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5358     a = (a + (a >> 4)) \& 0x0f0f0f0f; \textcolor{comment}{// max 8 per 4, now 8 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5359     a = (a + (a >> 8)); \textcolor{comment}{// max 16 per 8 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5360     a = (a + (a >> 16)); \textcolor{comment}{// max 32 per 8 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5361     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a \& 0xff;}

\DoxyCodeLine{5814     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((sz != 8) \&\& (sz != 15) \&\& (sz != 16) \&\& (sz != 24) \&\& (sz != 32)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} errorEnd;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5815 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5816     res = 1; \textcolor{comment}{// if we got this far, everything's good and we can return 1 instead of 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5817 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5818 errorEnd:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5819     stbi\_\_rewind(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5820     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} res;}

\DoxyCodeLine{5823 \textcolor{comment}{// read 16bit value and convert to 24bit RGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5824 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_tga\_read\_rgb16(stbi\_\_context* s, stbi\_uc* out)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5825 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5826     stbi\_\_uint16 px = (stbi\_\_uint16)stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5827     stbi\_\_uint16 fiveBitMask = 31;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5828     \textcolor{comment}{// we have 3 channels with 5bits each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5829     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r = (px >> 10) \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5830     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} g = (px >> 5) \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5831     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b = px \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5832     \textcolor{comment}{// Note that this saves the data in RGB(A) order, so it doesn't need to be swapped later}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5833     out[0] = (stbi\_uc)((r * 255) / 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5834     out[1] = (stbi\_uc)((g * 255) / 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5835     out[2] = (stbi\_uc)((b * 255) / 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5836 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5837     \textcolor{comment}{// some people claim that the most significant bit might be used for alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5838     \textcolor{comment}{// (possibly if an alpha-\/bit is set in the "{}image descriptor byte"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5839     \textcolor{comment}{// but that only made 16bit test images completely translucent..}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5840     \textcolor{comment}{// so let's treat all 15 and 16bit TGAs as RGB with no alpha.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6066 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_psd\_decode\_rle(stbi\_\_context* s, stbi\_uc* p, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pixelCount)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6067 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6068     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, nleft, len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6069 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6070     count = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6071     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((nleft = pixelCount -\/ count) > 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6072         len = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6073         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len == 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6074             \textcolor{comment}{// No-\/op.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6075         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6076         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len < 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6077             \textcolor{comment}{// Copy next len+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6078             len++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6079             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > nleft) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6080             count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6081             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6082                 *p = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6083                 p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6084                 len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6085             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6086         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6087         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6088             stbi\_uc   val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6089             \textcolor{comment}{// Next -\/len+1 bytes in the dest are replicated from next source byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6090             \textcolor{comment}{// (Interpret len as a negative 8-\/bit int.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6091             len = 257 -\/ len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6092             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > nleft) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6093             val = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6094             count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6095             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6096                 *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6097                 p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6098                 len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6099             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6100         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6101     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6102 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6103     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6104 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6105 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6106 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* stbi\_\_psd\_load(stbi\_\_context* s, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* x, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* y, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* comp, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp, stbi\_\_result\_info* ri, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bpc)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6107 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6108     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pixelCount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6109     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channelCount, compression;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6110     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channel, i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6111     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bitdepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6112     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6113     stbi\_uc* out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6114     STBI\_NOTUSED(ri);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6115 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6116     \textcolor{comment}{// Check identifier}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6117     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get32be(s) != 0x38425053)   \textcolor{comment}{// "{}8BPS"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6118         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}not PSD"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6119 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6120     \textcolor{comment}{// Check file type version.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6121     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get16be(s) != 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6122         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong version"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unsupported version of PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6123 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6124     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip 6 reserved bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6125     stbi\_\_skip(s, 6);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6126 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6127     \textcolor{comment}{// Read the number of channels (R, G, B, A, etc).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6128     channelCount = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6129     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channelCount < 0 || channelCount > 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6130         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong channel count"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unsupported number of channels in PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6131 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6132     \textcolor{comment}{// Read the rows and columns of the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6133     h = stbi\_\_get32be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6134     w = stbi\_\_get32be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6135 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6136     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (h > STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Very large image (corrupt?)"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6137     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (w > STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Very large image (corrupt?)"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6138 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6139     \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the depth is 8 bits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6140     bitdepth = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6141     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth != 8 \&\& bitdepth != 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6142         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}unsupported bit depth"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD bit depth is not 8 or 16 bit"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6143 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6144     \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the color mode is RGB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6145     \textcolor{comment}{// Valid options are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6146     \textcolor{comment}{//   0: Bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6147     \textcolor{comment}{//   1: Grayscale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6148     \textcolor{comment}{//   2: Indexed color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6149     \textcolor{comment}{//   3: RGB color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6150     \textcolor{comment}{//   4: CMYK color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6151     \textcolor{comment}{//   7: Multichannel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6152     \textcolor{comment}{//   8: Duotone}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6153     \textcolor{comment}{//   9: Lab color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6154     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get16be(s) != 3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6155         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong color format"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD is not in RGB color format"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6156 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6157     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the Mode Data.  (It's the palette for indexed color; other info for other modes.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6158     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{6159 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6160     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the image resources.  (resolution, pen tool paths, etc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6161     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{6162 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6163     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the reserved data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6164     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{6165 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6166     \textcolor{comment}{// Find out if the data is compressed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6167     \textcolor{comment}{// Known values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6168     \textcolor{comment}{//   0: no compression}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6169     \textcolor{comment}{//   1: RLE compressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6170     compression = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6171     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression > 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6172         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad compression"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD has an unknown compression format"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6173 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6174     \textcolor{comment}{// Check size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6175     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_mad3sizes\_valid(4, w, h, 0))}

\DoxyCodeLine{6177 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6178     \textcolor{comment}{// Create the destination image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6179 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6180     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!compression \&\& bitdepth == 16 \&\& bpc == 16) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{6182         ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel = 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6183     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6184     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6185         out = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(4 * w * h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6186 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6187     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!out) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}outofmem"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Out of memory"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6188     pixelCount = w * h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6189 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6190     \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize the data to zero.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6191     \textcolor{comment}{//memset( out, 0, pixelCount * 4 );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6192 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6193     \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, the image data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6194     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6195         \textcolor{comment}{// RLE as used by .PSD and .TIFF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6196         \textcolor{comment}{// Loop until you get the number of unpacked bytes you are expecting:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6197         \textcolor{comment}{//     Read the next source byte into n.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6198         \textcolor{comment}{//     If n is between 0 and 127 inclusive, copy the next n+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6199         \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is between -\/127 and -\/1 inclusive, copy the next byte -\/n+1 times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6200         \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is 128, noop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6201         \textcolor{comment}{// Endloop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6202 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6203         \textcolor{comment}{// The RLE-\/compressed data is preceded by a 2-\/byte data count for each row in the data,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6204         \textcolor{comment}{// which we're going to just skip.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6205         stbi\_\_skip(s, h * channelCount * 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6206 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6207         \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6208         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6209             stbi\_uc* p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6210 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6211             p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6212             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6213                 \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6214                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6215                     *p = (channel == 3 ? 255 : 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6216             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6217             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6218                 \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6220                     STBI\_FREE(out);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6221                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}corrupt"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad RLE data"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6222                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6223             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6224         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6225 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6226     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6227     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6228         \textcolor{comment}{// We're at the raw image data.  It's each channel in order (Red, Green, Blue, Alpha, ...)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6229         \textcolor{comment}{// where each channel consists of an 8-\/bit (or 16-\/bit) value for each pixel in the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6230 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6231         \textcolor{comment}{// Read the data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6232         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6233             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6234                 \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6235                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth == 16 \&\& bpc == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6236                     stbi\_\_uint16* q = ((stbi\_\_uint16*)out) + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6237                     stbi\_\_uint16 val = channel == 3 ? 65535 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6238                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, q += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6239                         *q = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6240                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6241                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6242                     stbi\_uc* p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6243                     stbi\_uc val = channel == 3 ? 255 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6244                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6245                         *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6246                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6247             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6248             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6249                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16) \{    \textcolor{comment}{// output bpc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6250                     stbi\_\_uint16* q = ((stbi\_\_uint16*)out) + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6251                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, q += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6252                         *q = (stbi\_\_uint16)stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6253                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6254                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6255                     stbi\_uc* p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6256                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth == 16) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// input bpc}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6260                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{6263                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6264                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6265             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6266         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6267     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6268 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6269     \textcolor{comment}{// remove weird white matte from PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6270     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channelCount >= 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6271         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6272             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w * h; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6273                 stbi\_\_uint16* pixel = (stbi\_\_uint16*)out + 4 * i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6274                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pixel[3] != 0 \&\& pixel[3] != 65535) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6275                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = pixel[3] / 65535.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6276                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ra = 1.0f / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6277                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_a = 65535.0f * (1 -\/ ra);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6278                     pixel[0] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[0] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6279                     pixel[1] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[1] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6280                     pixel[2] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[2] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6281                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6282             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6283         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6284         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6285             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w * h; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6286                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* pixel = out + 4 * i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6287                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pixel[3] != 0 \&\& pixel[3] != 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6288                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = pixel[3] / 255.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6289                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ra = 1.0f / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6290                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_a = 255.0f * (1 -\/ ra);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6291                     pixel[0] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[0] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6292                     pixel[1] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[1] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6293                     pixel[2] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[2] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6294                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6295             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6296         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6297     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6298 }

\DoxyCodeLine{6309     *y = h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6310     *x = w;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6712                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} g-\/>out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6713             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6714             -\/-\/len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6715             bits |= (stbi\_\_int32)stbi\_\_get8(s) << valid\_bits;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6716             valid\_bits += 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6717         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6718         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6719             stbi\_\_int32 code = bits \& codemask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6720             bits >>= codesize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6721             valid\_bits -\/= codesize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6722             \textcolor{comment}{// @OPTIMIZE: is there some way we can accelerate the non-\/clear path?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6723             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code == clear) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// clear code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6724                 codesize = lzw\_cs + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6725                 codemask = (1 << codesize) -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6726                 avail = clear + 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6727                 oldcode = -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6728                 first = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6729             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6730             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code == clear + 1) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// end of stream code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6731                 stbi\_\_skip(s, len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6732                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((len = stbi\_\_get8(s)) > 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6733                     stbi\_\_skip(s, len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6734                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} g-\/>out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6735             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6736             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code <= avail) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6737                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (first) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6738                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}no clear code"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6739                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6740 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6741                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (oldcode >= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6742                     p = \&g-\/>codes[avail++];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6743                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (avail > 8192) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6744                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too many codes"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6745                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6746 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6747                     p-\/>prefix = (stbi\_\_int16)oldcode;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6748                     p-\/>first = g-\/>codes[oldcode].first;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6749                     p-\/>suffix = (code == avail) ? p-\/>first : g-\/>codes[code].first;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6750                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6751                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code == avail)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6752                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}illegal code in raster"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6753 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6754                 stbi\_\_out\_gif\_code(g, (stbi\_\_uint16)code);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6755 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6756                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((avail \& codemask) == 0 \&\& avail <= 0x0FFF) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6757                     codesize++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6758                     codemask = (1 << codesize) -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6759                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6760 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6761                 oldcode = code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6762             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6763             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6764                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}illegal code in raster"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6765             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6766         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6767     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6768 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6769 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6770 \textcolor{comment}{// this function is designed to support animated gifs, although stb\_image doesn't support it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6771 \textcolor{comment}{// two back is the image from two frames ago, used for a very specific disposal format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6772 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc* stbi\_\_gif\_load\_next(stbi\_\_context* s, stbi\_\_gif* g, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* comp, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp, stbi\_uc* two\_back)}

\DoxyCodeLine{6774     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} dispose;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6780     \textcolor{comment}{// on first frame, any non-\/written pixels get the background colour (non-\/transparent)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6783         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_gif\_header(s, g, comp, 0)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_\_g\_failure\_reason set by stbi\_\_gif\_header}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6786         pcount = g-\/>w * g-\/>h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6787         g-\/>out = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(4 * pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6788         g-\/>background = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(4 * pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6789         g-\/>history = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6790         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!g-\/>out || !g-\/>background || !g-\/>history)}

\DoxyCodeLine{6792 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6793         \textcolor{comment}{// image is treated as "{}transparent"{} at the start -\/ ie, nothing overwrites the current background;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6794         \textcolor{comment}{// background colour is only used for pixels that are not rendered first frame, after that "{}background"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6795         \textcolor{comment}{// color refers to the color that was there the previous frame.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6796         memset(g-\/>out, 0x00, 4 * pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6797         memset(g-\/>background, 0x00, 4 * pcount); \textcolor{comment}{// state of the background (starts transparent)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6798         memset(g-\/>history, 0x00, pcount);        \textcolor{comment}{// pixels that were affected previous frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6799         first\_frame = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6800     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6801     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6802         \textcolor{comment}{// second frame -\/ how do we dispose of the previous one?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6803         dispose = (g-\/>eflags \& 0x1C) >> 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6804         pcount = g-\/>w * g-\/>h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6805 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6806         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((dispose == 3) \&\& (two\_back == 0)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6807             dispose = 2; \textcolor{comment}{// if I don't have an image to revert back to, default to the old background}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6808         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6809 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6810         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dispose == 3) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// use previous graphic}}

\DoxyCodeLine{7026                     two\_back = out -\/ 2 * stride;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7027                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7028 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7029                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (delays) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7030                     (*delays)[layers -\/ 1U] = g.delay;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7031                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7032             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7033         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (u != 0);}

\DoxyCodeLine{7036         STBI\_FREE(g.out);}
\DoxyCodeLine{7037         STBI\_FREE(g.history);}
\DoxyCodeLine{7038         STBI\_FREE(g.background);}
\DoxyCodeLine{7039 }

\DoxyCodeLine{7041         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp \&\& req\_comp != 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7042             out = stbi\_\_convert\_format(out, 4, req\_comp, layers * g.w, g.h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{7043 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7044         *z = layers;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7045         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7046     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7047     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7048         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}not GIF"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Image was not as a gif type."{}});}

\DoxyCodeLine{7136 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_hdr\_convert(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}* output, stbi\_uc* input, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7137 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7138     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (input[3] != 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7139         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7140         \textcolor{comment}{// Exponent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7141         f1 = (float)ldexp(1.0f, input[3] -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})(128 + 8));}
\DoxyCodeLine{7142         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp <= 2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7143             output[0] = (input[0] + input[1] + input[2]) * f1 / 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7144         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7145             output[0] = input[0] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7146             output[1] = input[1] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7147             output[2] = input[2] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7148         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7149         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp == 2) output[1] = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7150         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp == 4) output[3] = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7151     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7152     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7153         \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (req\_comp) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7154         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 4: output[3] = 1; \textcolor{comment}{/* fallthrough */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7155         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 3: output[0] = output[1] = output[2] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7156             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{7157         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 2: output[1] = 1; \textcolor{comment}{/* fallthrough */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7158         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 1: output[0] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7159             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{7160         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7161     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7162 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7163 }
